<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Biographies">Biographies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Joseph_Priestley&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Biographies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r853264625" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="refbegin" style="">
<p>The most exhaustive biography of Priestley is Robert Schofield's recent two-volume work; several one-volume treatments exist, all somewhat older: Gibbs, Holt and Thorpe. Graham and Smith focus on Priestley's life in America and Uglow and Jackson both discuss Priestley's life in the context of other developments in science.
</p>
<ul><li>Gibbs, F. W. <i>Joseph Priestley: Adventurer in Science and Champion of Truth</i>. London: Thomas Nelson and Sons, 1965.</li>
<li>Graham, Jenny. <i>Revolutionary in Exile: The Emigration of Joseph Priestley to America, 1794–1804.</i> <i>Transactions of the American Philosophical Society</i> 85 (1995). <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-87169-852-8" title="Special:BookSources/0-87169-852-8">0-87169-852-8</a>.</li>
<li>Holt, Anne. <i>A Life of Joseph Priestley</i>. London: Oxford University Press, 1931.</li>
<li>Jackson, Joe. <i>A World on Fire: A Heretic, an Aristocrat and the Race to Discover Oxygen</i>. New York: Viking, 2005. <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-670-03434-7" title="Special:BookSources/0-670-03434-7">0-670-03434-7</a>.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Steven_Berlin_Johnson" title="Steven Berlin Johnson">Johnson, Steven</a>. <i>The Invention of Air: A Story of Science, Faith, Revolution, and the Birth of America</i>. New York: Riverhead, 2008. <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/1-59448-852-5" title="Special:BookSources/1-59448-852-5">1-59448-852-5</a>.</li>
<li>Schofield, Robert E. <i>The Enlightenment of Joseph Priestley: A Study of his Life and Work from 1733 to 1773</i>. University Park: Pennsylvania State University Press, 1997. <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-271-01662-0" title="Special:BookSources/0-271-01662-0">0-271-01662-0</a>.</li>
<li>Schofield, Robert E. <i>The Enlightened Joseph Priestley: A Study of His Life and Work from 1773 to 1804</i>. University Park: Pennsylvania State University Press, 2004. <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-271-02459-3" title="Special:BookSources/0-271-02459-3">0-271-02459-3</a>.</li>
<li>Smith, Edgar F. <i><a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?vid=OCLC00538529&amp;id=eyQFAAAAMAAJ" rel="nofollow">Priestley in America, 1794–1804</a></i>. Philadelphia: P. Blakiston's Son and Co., 1920.</li>
<li>Tapper, Alan. "Joseph Priestley". <i>Dictionary of Literary Biography</i> 252: <i>British Philosophers 1500–1799</i>. Eds. Philip B. Dematteis and Peter S. Fosl. Detroit: Gale Group, 2002.</li>
<li>Thorpe, T. E. <i><a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/josephpriestley01thorgoog" rel="nofollow">Joseph Priestley</a></i>. London: J. M. Dent, 1906.</li>
<li>Uglow, Jenny. <i>The Lunar Men: Five Friends Whose Curiosity Changed the World</i>. New York: Farrar, Straus and Giroux, 2002. <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-374-19440-8" title="Special:BookSources/0-374-19440-8">0-374-19440-8</a>.</li></ul>
